[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspec. Some types[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m are no profiles holding them. The programmer can also extend this list by [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefining his own types[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m by using the appropriate plug-in. There are three types of plug ins regarding[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto define new types[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m and the third one is very specific: allows to extend the number of elements [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m elements special type.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m756[0m[39m:    const char* PreMaj;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m757[0m[39m:    const char* PostMaj;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m758[0m[39m:    const char* PreMin, *PostMin;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m759[0m[39m:    cmsStage* mpe;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m760[0m[39m:        [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m761[0m[39m:    mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m762[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m763[0m[39m:    switch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m764[0m[39m:    case [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m765[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"[0m[32m[[0m[32m /CIEBasedDEF\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m766[0m[39m:        PreMaj = [0m[32m"<"[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m767[0m[39m:        PostMaj = [0m[32m">\n"[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m768[0m[39m:        PreMin = PostMin = [0m[32m""[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m769[0m[39m:        break;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m770[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m771[0m[39m:    case [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m772[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"[0m[32m[[0m[32m /CIEBasedDEFG\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m773[0m[39m:        PreMaj = [0m[32m"[0m[32m[[0m[32m"[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m774[0m[39m:        PostMaj = [0m[32m"[0m[32m][0m[32m\n"[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/cmslut.[0m[1;92mc:1228[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1232[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m1228:c[0m[39mmsStageSignature CMSEXPORT [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst cmsStage* mpe[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1229[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1230[0m[39m:    return mpe -> Type;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1231[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1232[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/cmstypes.[0m[1;92mc:208[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m216[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m208[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To deal with position tables[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m209[0m[39m:typedef cmsBool [0m[1;39m([0m[39m* PositionTableEntryFn[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct _cms_typehandler_struct* self,[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m210[0m[39m:                                             cmsIOHANDLER* io,[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m211[0m[39m:                                             void* Cargo,[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m212[0m[39m:                                             cmsUInt32Number n,[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m213[0m[39m:                                             cmsUInt32Number SizeOfTag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m214[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m215[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Helper function to deal with position tables as described in ICC spec [0m[1;36m4.3[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m216[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m A table of n elements is read, where first comes n records containing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets and sizes and[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The crash is a null-pointer dereference in cmsStageType [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset [0m[1;36m0x8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, invoked by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEmitCIEBasedDEF via calls to cmsStageInputChannels, cmsStageType and subsequent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstage-field accesses. These functions assume that Pipeline->Elements [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe head of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe cmsStage linked list[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is non-NULL, but malformed or incomplete inputs can [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduce an empty cmsPipeline, leaving [0m[33mElements[0m[39m==NULL. Calling [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcmsStageInputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on a NULL `mpe` triggers the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobserved SEGV.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Locations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The critical code is in src/cmsps2.c:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - EmitCIEBasedDEF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m754[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m775[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - WriteInputLUT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcaller of EmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptionally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m other functions in the PostScript CSA generation pipeline that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly dereference Pipeline->Elements.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Add a null-guard in EmitCIEBasedDEF before any dereference of [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline->Elements`:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsIOHANDLER* m, cmsPipeline* Pipeline, cmsUInt32Number [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIntent, cmsCIEXYZ* BlackPoint[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against empty pipelines[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Gracefully abort PostScript CIEBasedDEF emission[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FALSE [0m[35m/[0m[39m error[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         cmsStage* mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[33m...[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Ensure WriteInputLUT handles EmitCIEBasedDEF’s failure code:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int [0m[1;35mWriteInputLUT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsIOHANDLER* m, cmsPipeline* Pipeline, cmsUInt32Number [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIntent, cmsCIEXYZ* BlackPoint[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Early guard if pipeline has no stages[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mEmitCIEBasedDEF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, Pipeline, Intent, BlackPoint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m abort further LUT emission[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Existing code for shaper tables, matrix, etc.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[33m...[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Optionally, perform a similar check at the entry of GenerateCSA or even at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe top-level API [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsGetPostScriptColorResource [0m[35m/[0m[39m cmsGetPostScriptCSA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to catch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty pipelines early:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     cmsHPROFILE [0m[1;35mcmsGetPostScriptCSA[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[33m...[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         cmsPipeline* Pipeline = [0m[1;35mBuildPipelineFromTransform[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineGetPtrToFirstStage[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mcmsPipelineFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return NULL;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m no CSA generated[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[33m...[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation of Behavior  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Prevents Null-Deref**: By validating Pipeline and its Elements pointer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore any field access, we eliminate the crash path.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Graceful Degradation**: Returning [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m or NULL signals to the caller that CSA [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgeneration failed, rather than crashing. Existing callers already check for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzero/non-zero or NULL return values when writing out PostScript resources.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**: We do not alter external libraries, harness code, or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests. All changes are confined to the PostScript generation module. The core [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpipeline and stage logic remain untouched for valid inputs.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Consistent Error Handling**: All emission functions in cmsps2.c already [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn int success flags, so adding failure returns aligns with existing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconventions. No broad try-catch or suppression of other errors.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Empty/Invalid Pipeline Cases**: Now cause CSA generation to abort earlier. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDownstream code must handle a NULL or zero-length resource. Tests expecting an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty but non-crashing output will continue to pass.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Logging**: If desired, we can augment the guard with a cmsSignalError call [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto record an internal error, but it’s not strictly required for correctness.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Propagation**: By aborting in WriteInputLUT and EmitCIEBasedDEF, we ensure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat later PostScript sections [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., shaper definitions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m aren’t emitted with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbogus pipeline.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar In-Code Patterns  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - scanf-style readers in cmstypes.c guard their io context and array pointers [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore usage. Aligning EmitCIEBasedDEF’s guard with these existing patterns [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintains internal consistency.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other modules in lcms check for NULL handlers or empty tables before [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing. Following the same motif in cmsps2.c preserves architectural style.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Harness or Test Modifications  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter any fuzzing harness or existing test suite. The fix strictly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures that malformed or empty pipelines do not cause uncontrolled dereferences in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe PostScript CSA generator.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith this strategy, valid pipelines continue unaffected, while null/empty pipelines[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail gracefully without segmentation faults.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalled from `EmitCIEBasedDEF` after advancing the `mpe` pointer.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Analysis shows that if the pipeline contains only a curve-set stage, the code [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskips that stage [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mpe = mpe->Next;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and ends up with `mpe == NULL`. The [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent unguarded `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` dereferences this NULL pointer, triggering[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SEGV.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code is intended to emit a “CIEBasedDEF” PostScript resource only when [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth an initial curve-set stage and a CLUT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolor lookup table[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stage are present. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For pipelines that lack a CLUT stage, the correct behavior is to return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mi.e., no CIEBasedDEF emitted[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current logic already returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m in the `switch` default [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsupported channel [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcounts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and at the end if the stage type is not CLUT—but it fails to handle the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL case.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed patch in `src/cmsps2.c`—function `EmitCIEBasedDEF`  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Make the curve-skipping loop safe by guarding the loop condition on `mpe`:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m write curve [0m[33m...[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          mpe = mpe->Next;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Change to:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m write curve [0m[33m...[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          mpe = mpe->Next;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after the loop, check for NULL and return early:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Finally, guard the CLUT check on a non-NULL `mpe`:  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m emit CLUT [0m[33m...[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why this approach is optimal  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It addresses the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL `mpe` pointer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m directly while preserving the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting stage-emission logic.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pipelines without a CLUT stage will correctly short-circuit and return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching existing behavior for non-[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-channel pipelines.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external or harness code is modified; only `cmsps2.c` is updated.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal change avoids over-catching errors and keeps exception cases [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side effects and mitigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pipelines that legitimately contain an initial curve-set but no CLUT will now [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanly return without a CIEBasedDEF—previous code would crash instead.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change in output is made for valid pipelines with both curve and CLUT [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstages.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests exercising CIEBasedDEF with proper pipelines should continue to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass unaffected.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar safety guards exist elsewhere in color-processing code where stage [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlists are iterated—mirroring those patterns ensures consistency.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No additional patching of utility functions or harness code is needed.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplying the patch, the build failed during linking with an undefined reference to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`WriteCurveSet`, indicating that the patch introduced calls to a symbol that is not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefined or not exposed in the current compilation units.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• A fuzzing run of `cms_postscript_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibFuzzer, ASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on an input [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m` caused a crash:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‑ AddressSanitizer reported a SEGV on a read from address [0m[1;36m0x8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull page[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‑ The top of the stack trace points to `cmsStageType` in [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lcms/src/cmslut.[0m[1;92mc:1230:19[0m[39m`, indicating a null‐pointer dereference when inspecting [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma stage in a pipeline.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‑ The crash chain is: `cmsStageType` → `EmitCIEBasedDEF` → `WriteInputLUT` → [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GenerateCSA` → `cmsGetPostScriptColorResource` → `cmsGetPostScriptCSA` → the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer entrypoint.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Observations from the Crash Log[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The error arises when the code assumes a non‐NULL `Pipeline` and non‐NULL [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline->Elements`.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• No preliminary checks guard the dereference of `mpe = Pipeline->Elements` or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent calls that expect `mpe` to be valid.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The crash is reproducible in “interactive” mode with libFuzzer, running a single [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m times.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch modifies `EmitCIEBasedDEF` in `src/cmsps2.c`:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Adds an early return if `Pipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Introduces local variable initialization:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     cmsStage* mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Wraps each `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call in a null check:  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Inserts calls to `WriteCurveSet` within the guarded blocks to handle curve‐set [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstages.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Result[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, the build in `utils/psicc` fails at link time:[0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• The linker error occurs in `cmsps2.o` within the function [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cmsGetPostScriptColorResource`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• No definition or export of `WriteCurveSet` is found in the patched sources or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlinked libraries, leading to a failure to produce the `psicc` binary.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the introduction of the undefined `WriteCurveSet` symbol:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any calls to `WriteCurveSet` and associated `cmsStageType` checks [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced in the last patch attempt. These calls have no implementation or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration in the current codebase and are the direct cause of the linker failure.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add robust null‐pointer guards in `EmitCIEBasedDEF` to prevent null [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdereferences:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the very start of `EmitCIEBasedDEF` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore any use of `Pipeline` or its [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmembers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPipeline == NULL || Pipeline->Elements == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace the existing two‐step declaration and assignment of `mpe` with a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle guarded initialization:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      cmsStage* mpe = Pipeline->Elements;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSince we have already ensured `Pipeline->Elements` is non‐NULL, `mpe` is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguaranteed valid here.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Guard every subsequent call to `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with an `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern ensures that even if the pipeline is malformed or partially [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated, we never call into `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. For example:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"/DecodeDEF [0m[32m[[0m[32m "[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mEmitNGamma[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[1;35mcmsStageOutputChannels[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[1;35m_cmsStageGetPtrToCurveSet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"[0m[32m][0m[32m\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         mpe = mpe->Next;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"/Table "[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mWriteCLUT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, mpe, PreMaj, PostMaj, PreMin, PostMin,[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   FALSE, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsColorSpaceSignature[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35m_cmsIOPrintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, [0m[32m"[0m[32m][0m[32m\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         mpe = mpe->Next;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve existing PostScript‐emission logic by leveraging the already‐defined [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic `EmitNGamma` for curve‐set stages:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do **not** introduce any new curve‐set writer function. The existing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EmitNGamma` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwrapped by the `[0m[35m/[0m[95mDecodeDEF[0m[39m` block[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m correctly emits the gamma curves [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom a `cmsSigCurveSetElemType` stage.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Audit other use sites of `Pipeline->Elements` within `cmsps2.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`WriteInputLUT` and `GenerateCSA`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure they either rely on the same guard in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EmitCIEBasedDEF` or have their own null‐checks if they dereference `Pipeline` or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline->Elements` directly.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any further unguarded dereferences exist, apply the same pattern: check for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NULL` before usage.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verify build and linking:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After removing `WriteCurveSet` calls, the undefined‐symbol linker error will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe resolved.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that no residual references to `WriteCurveSet` remain in any [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation unit.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Regression testing:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the existing test suite and fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`cms_postscript_fuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No SEGV from null pipelines in `cmsStageType`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Correct PostScript output behavior for valid pipelines.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No new linker or compile errors introduced.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-------------[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The root‐cause of the null dereference is the unconditional use of [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Pipeline->Elements` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand subsequent `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without guarding against [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NULL`. Introducing early exit checks fully addresses the SEGV by never allowing a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NULL` stage pointer to be dereferenced.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The undefined symbol `WriteCurveSet` is a byproduct of the last patch attempt and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas no implementation in the codebase. Removing it restores link correctness [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout sacrificing any existing functionality.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By reusing the existing `EmitNGamma` implementation, we maintain the intended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcurve‐set output logic. No new external dependencies or alterations to harness or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest code are needed.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrapping all `cmsStageType` calls in `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is minimal, precise, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not alter the behavior for well-formed pipelines.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This strategy ensures that the fix applies cleanly to the **initial** codebase [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mreapplying only necessary guards[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and that no external libraries, harness, or test[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode are modified.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m------------------------------------[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Early returns in `EmitCIEBasedDEF` for empty or malformed pipelines will skip [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPostScript emission. This matches the intended fail-safe behavior and should not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisrupt consumers expecting a zero return to indicate “nothing emitted.”[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If future pipeline stages rely on `EmitCIEBasedDEF` side effects, they must [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandle a zero return. Current downstream callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `WriteInputLUT`, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GenerateCSA`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already check return values and propagate errors, so no additional [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges are required.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing pipeline definitions with valid stages remain fully supported, and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcurve‐set output continues unchanged via `EmitNGamma`.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReferences in Codebase[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m----------------------[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing static function `EmitNGamma` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `cmsps2.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for curve‐set stage output.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Static function `WriteCLUT` in `cmsps2.c` for CLUT stages.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other null‐checking patterns in `OutputValueSampler` for safe dereferencing.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
